Comprehensive articles on Wookieepedia

A Comprehensive article is an article that adheres to quality standards, but cannot reach [Good status](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Good_articles "Wookieepedia:Good articles") due to its limited content. At present, there are **9,244** Comprehensive articles, out of a total of 214,729 articles on Wookieepedia. Articles that no longer meet the criteria can be proposed for improvement or removal at the [Comprehensive article reviews](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Comprehensive_article_reviews "Wookieepedia:Comprehensive article reviews") page.

A small circular icon ([![CA-Icon](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/CA-Icon.svg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/16?cb=20240801064129)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e4/CA-Icon.svg/revision/latest?cb=20240801064129)) in the top right corner of an article's page indicates that the article has achieved Comprehensive status.

[EduCorps](/wiki/Wookieepedia:EduCorps "Wookieepedia:EduCorps"), see the [Canon](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Comprehensive_articles/Canon "Wookieepedia:Comprehensive articles/Canon"), [Legends](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Comprehensive_articles/Legends "Wookieepedia:Comprehensive articles/Legends"), and [OOU](/wiki/Wookieepedia:Comprehensive_articles/OOU "Wookieepedia:Comprehensive articles/OOU") subpages for listing purposes.

* [Legends](#)
